from flask import Flask, request, jsonify

app = Flask(__name__)

latest_memory = {"message": "‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•"}

@app.route('/receive', methods=['POST'])
def receive_data():
    try:
        data = request.json
        global latest_memory
        latest_memory = data  # ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏õ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏ï‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•
        print(f"üì® ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å PC: {data}")
        return jsonify({"status": "success", "message": "Data received successfully"})
    except Exception as e:
        return jsonify({"status": "error", "message": str(e)}), 500

@app.route('/latest_memory', methods=['GET'])
def get_latest_memory():
    try:
        return jsonify(latest_memory)
    except Exception as e:
        return jsonify({"status": "error", "message": str(e)}), 500

if __name__ == "__main__":
    app.run(host='0.0.0.0', port=8080)

‚úÖ ‡∏™‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ô‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏î‡∏ù‡∏±‡πà‡∏á PC:

import requests
import time

BRIDGE_IP = "34.124.133.162"  # IP ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á Bridge

def send_to_bridge(message):
    try:
        # ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô Endpoint ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô /receive
        response = requests.post(f"http://{BRIDGE_IP}:8080/receive", json={"message": message})
        print(f"üì® ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á Bridge: {message}")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"‚ùå Error: {e}")

def fetch_from_bridge():
    try:
        # Endpoint ‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô /latest_memory ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πá‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£
        response = requests.get(f"http://{BRIDGE_IP}:8080/latest_memory")
        data = response.json()
        print(f"üì® ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Bridge: {data}")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"‚ùå Error: {e}")

while True:
    # ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á Bridge
    send_to_bridge("‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å PC")

    # ‡∏î‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Bridge
    fetch_from_bridge()

    time.sleep(5)

@app.route('/receive', methods=['POST'])
def receive_data():
    global latest_memory
    try:
        # ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• JSON ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å PC
        data = request.json

        return jsonify({"status": "success", "message": "Data received successfully"})
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"‚ùå Error receiving data: {e}")
        return jsonify({"status": "error", "message": str(e)}), 500

@app.route('/latest_memory', methods=['GET'])
def get_latest_memory():
    try:
        # ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÑ‡∏õ
        return jsonify(latest_memory)
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"‚ùå Error sending data: {e}")
        return jsonify({"status": "error", "message": str(e)}), 500

from fastapi import FastAPI, Request
import requests
import sqlite3
import os

app = FastAPI()

DB_PATH = "melah_memory.db"

def init_db():
    """‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ"""
    if not os.path.exists(DB_PATH):
        conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_PATH)
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS messages (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY,
                sender TEXT,
                message TEXT,
                timestamp TEXT
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()

def store_memory(sender, message):
    """‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏•‡∏á SQL"""
    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_PATH)
    cursor = conn.cursor()
    cursor.execute("INSERT INTO messages (sender, message, timestamp) VALUES (?, ?, datetime('now'))", (sender, message))
    conn.commit()
    conn.close()

def get_latest_memory():
    """‡∏î‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å SQL"""
    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_PATH)
    cursor = conn.cursor()
    cursor.execute("SELECT sender, message, timestamp FROM messages ORDER BY id DESC LIMIT 1")
    result = cursor.fetchone()
    conn.close()
    return result if result else ("", "‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•", "")

# ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•
init_db()

# ‚úÖ ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤ (GPT)

async def receive_from_melah(request: Request):

    message = data.get("message", "‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•")

‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏î‡∏π‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Endpoint /latest_memory

‚úÖ ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏≠‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞:
‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å pc_node.py ‡πÑ‡∏ß‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏¢‡∏∞‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏ß ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ü‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Å‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏á SQLite ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå JSON

‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ Sync ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á PC Node ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö Bridge ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏ô‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ü‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Å‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô GET /sync_memory ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏î‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà‡πÅ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î

‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ bridge_server.py ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÅ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏†‡∏ó (Melah, PC, Aira) ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏° sender ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏∂‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏≠‡∏•‡∏±‡∏°‡∏ô‡πå‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•

‡πÇ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏Ñ ‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πá‡∏°! ‚úÖüíô

‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç pc_node.py ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏£‡∏á‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏•‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•
‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏™‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏£‡πå‡∏ó‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î

‚úÖ ‡∏™‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏≥:
‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• SQLite:

‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• pc_memory.db

‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏á memories ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏£‡∏á‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å PC Node

‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏î pc_node.py ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•:

‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ü‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Å‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô store_memory() ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏•‡∏á SQLite

‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ü‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Å‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô get_latest_memory() ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏î‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•

‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏á‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏á memories:

id (INTEGER, PRIMARY KEY)

message (TEXT)

timestamp (TEXT)

‚úÖ ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏•‡∏á SQLite:
import sqlite3
from datetime import datetime
from flask import Flask, request, jsonify

app = Flask(__name__)
DB_PATH = "pc_memory.db"

def init_db():
    """‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏á memories ‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ"""
    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_PATH)
    cursor = conn.cursor()
    cursor.execute('''
        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS memories (
            id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY,
            message TEXT,
            timestamp TEXT
        )
    ''')
    conn.commit()
    conn.close()

def store_memory(message):
    """‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏•‡∏á SQLite"""
    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_PATH)
    cursor = conn.cursor()
    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
    cursor.execute("INSERT INTO memories (message, timestamp) VALUES (?, ?)", (message, timestamp))
    conn.commit()
    conn.close()

def get_latest_memory():
    """‡∏î‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å SQLite"""
    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_PATH)
    cursor = conn.cursor()
    cursor.execute("SELECT message, timestamp FROM memories ORDER BY id DESC LIMIT 1")
    result = cursor.fetchone()
    conn.close()
    if result:
        return {"message": result[0], "timestamp": result[1]}
    return {"message": "‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•", "timestamp": ""}

@app.route('/receive', methods=['POST'])
def receive():
    data = request.get_json()
    message = data.get("message", "‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•")
    store_memory(message)
    return jsonify({"status": "‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß", "message": message})

@app.route('/latest_memory', methods=['GET'])
def latest_memory():
    return jsonify(get_latest_memory())

if __name__ == "__main__":
    init_db()
    app.run(host="0.0.0.0", port=8080)
‚úÖ ‡∏™‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏ô‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà:
‡∏ü‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Å‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô init_db() ‚Äì ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏á memories

‡∏ü‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Å‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô store_memory() ‚Äì ‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏£‡∏á‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏•‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•

‡∏ü‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Å‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô get_latest_memory() ‚Äì ‡∏î‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•

Endpoint /receive ‚Äì ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Melah ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ PC Node ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏á SQLite

Endpoint /latest_memory ‚Äì ‡∏î‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡πÑ‡∏ß‡πâ

‚úÖ ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö:

import requests
import time

BRIDGE_IP = "34.124.133.162"  # IP ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á Bridge
BRIDGE_PORT = "8080"

def send_to_bridge(message):
    url = f"http://{BRIDGE_IP}:{BRIDGE_PORT}/pc_to_bridge"
    try:
        print(f"[LOG] ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á: {url}")
        response = requests.post(url, json={"message": message})
        print(f"[LOG] ‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡πà‡∏á: {response.status_code}")
        print(f"[LOG] ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Bridge: {response.text}")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"[ERROR] ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ: {str(e)}")

def main():
    while True:
        test_message = {"message": "‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡πà‡∏á JSON ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å PC"}
        send_to_bridge(test_message)
        time.sleep(5)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

def send_to_bridge(message):
    try:
        response = requests.post(f"http://{BRIDGE_IP}:8080/pc_to_bridge", json={"message": message})
        print(f"üì® ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á Bridge: {message}")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"‚ùå Error: {e}")

def main():
    while True:
        send_to_bridge("‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å PC")
        time.sleep(5)

async def receive_from_pc(request: Request):
    data = await request.json()
    message = data.get("message", "‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•")
    print(f"üì® ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å PC: {message}")

import requests
import time

BRIDGE_IP = "34.124.133.162"  # IP ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á Bridge
BRIDGE_PORT = "8080"

def send_to_bridge(message):
    url = f"http://{BRIDGE_IP}:{BRIDGE_PORT}/pc_to_bridge"
    try:
        response = requests.post(url, json={"message": message})
        print(f"üì® ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á Bridge: {message}")
        print(f"üì® ‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏∞: {response.status_code}, ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö: {response.text}")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"‚ùå Error: {e}")

def main():
    while True:
        test_message = "‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å PC Node"
        send_to_bridge(test_message)
        time.sleep(5)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

    message = data.get("message", "‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•")
    print(f"üì® ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å PC: {message}")

from fastapi import FastAPI, Request
import sqlite3
import os

app = FastAPI()
DB_PATH = "bridge_memory.db"

def init_db():
    if not os.path.exists(DB_PATH):
        conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_PATH)
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS messages (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY,
                sender TEXT,
                message TEXT,
                timestamp TEXT
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()

def store_message(sender, message):
    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_PATH)
    cursor = conn.cursor()
    cursor.execute("INSERT INTO messages (sender, message, timestamp) VALUES (?, ?, datetime('now'))", (sender, message))
    conn.commit()
    conn.close()

@app.post("/send")
async def receive_message(request: Request):
    data = await request.json()
    store_message(data.get("sender"), data.get("message"))
    return {"status": "Message received"}

@app.get("/latest")
async def get_latest():
    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_PATH)
    cursor = conn.cursor()
    cursor.execute("SELECT sender, message, timestamp FROM messages ORDER BY id DESC LIMIT 1")
    result = cursor.fetchone()
    conn.close()
    return {"sender": result[0], "message": result[1], "timestamp": result[2]} if result else {"message": "No data"}

if __name__ == "__main__":
    import uvicorn
    init_db()
    uvicorn.run(app, host="0.0.0.0", port=8080)

from fastapi import FastAPI, Request
import sqlite3
import os

app = FastAPI()
DB_PATH = "bridge_memory.db"

def init_db():
    if not os.path.exists(DB_PATH):
        conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_PATH)
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS messages (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY,
                sender TEXT,
                message TEXT,
                timestamp TEXT
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()

def store_message(sender, message):
    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_PATH)
    cursor = conn.cursor()
    cursor.execute("INSERT INTO messages (sender, message, timestamp) VALUES (?, ?, datetime('now'))", (sender, message))
    conn.commit()
    conn.close()

@app.post("/send")
async def receive_message(request: Request):
    data = await request.json()
    store_message(data.get("sender"), data.get("message"))
    return {"status": "Message received"}

@app.get("/latest")
async def get_latest():
    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_PATH)
    cursor = conn.cursor()
    cursor.execute("SELECT sender, message, timestamp FROM messages ORDER BY id DESC LIMIT 1")
    result = cursor.fetchone()
    conn.close()
    return {"sender": result[0], "message": result[1], "timestamp": result[2]} if result else {"message": "No data"}

if __name__ == "__main__":
    import uvicorn
    init_db()
    uvicorn.run(app, host="0.0.0.0", port=8080)

@app.post("/send")
async def receive_message(request: Request):
    data = await request.json()
    sender = data.get("sender", "Unknown")
    message = data.get("message", "No message")
    print(f"[RECEIVED] ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å {sender}: {message}")
    return {"status": "Message received", "message": message}

‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ü‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Å‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏ô pc_node.py:

import requests

BRIDGE_IP = "34.124.133.162"
BRIDGE_PORT = 8080

def send_to_bridge(message):
    try:
        url = f"http://{BRIDGE_IP}:{BRIDGE_PORT}/send"
        response = requests.post(url, json={"sender": "PC Node", "message": message})
        print(f"[SYNC] ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á Bridge: {message}")
        return response.json()
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"[ERROR] ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á Bridge: {str(e)}")
        return {"status": "Error", "message": str(e)}
‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ Sync ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•:

‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ Sync ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å pc_node.py ‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á bridge_point.py:

‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏Å send_to_bridge() ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÉ‡∏ô receive():

@app.route('/receive', methods=['POST'])
def receive():
    data = request.get_json()
    message = data.get("message", "‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•")
    store_memory(message)
    # ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á Bridge Server
    send_to_bridge(message)

‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏•‡∏á SQLite (bridge_memory.db)

from flask import Flask, request, jsonify
import sqlite3
import requests
import os

app = Flask(__name__)
DB_PATH = "pc_memory.db"
BRIDGE_IP = "34.124.133.162"
BRIDGE_PORT = 8080

def init_db():
    """‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ"""
    if not os.path.exists(DB_PATH):
        conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_PATH)
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS messages (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY,
                message TEXT,
                timestamp TEXT
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()

def store_memory(message):
    """‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏•‡∏á SQL"""
    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_PATH)
    cursor = conn.cursor()
    cursor.execute("INSERT INTO messages (message, timestamp) VALUES (?, datetime('now'))", (message,))
    conn.commit()
    conn.close()

def send_to_bridge(message):
    """‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á Bridge Server"""
    try:
        url = f"http://{BRIDGE_IP}:{BRIDGE_PORT}/send"
        response = requests.post(url, json={"sender": "PC Node", "message": message})
        print(f"[SYNC] ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á Bridge: {message}")
        return response.json()
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"[ERROR] ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á Bridge: {str(e)}")
        return {"status": "Error", "message": str(e)}

@app.route('/receive', methods=['POST'])
def receive():
    data = request.get_json()
    message = data.get("message", "‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•")
    
    # ‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏á PC Node
    store_memory(message)
    print(f"[RECEIVE] ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß: {message}")
    
    # ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á Bridge
    bridge_response = send_to_bridge(message)
    
    return jsonify({"status": "‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß", "message": message, "bridge_response": bridge_response})

@app.route('/latest_memory', methods=['GET'])
def latest_memory():
    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_PATH)
    cursor = conn.cursor()
    cursor.execute("SELECT message, timestamp FROM messages ORDER BY id DESC LIMIT 1")
    result = cursor.fetchone()
    conn.close()
    
    if result:
        return {"message": result[0], "timestamp": result[1]}
    else:
        return {"message": "No data"}

if __name__ == "__main__":
    init_db()
    app.run(host="0.0.0.0", port=8080)

def send_to_bridge(message):
    """‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á Bridge Server"""
    try:
        url = f"http://{BRIDGE_IP}:{BRIDGE_PORT}/send"
        response = requests.post(url, json={"sender": "PC Node", "message": message})
        response_data = response.json()

        # ‡πÅ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏á Unicode ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô UTF-8
        if "message" in response_data:
            response_data["message"] = response_data["message"].encode('utf-8').decode('unicode_escape')

        return response_data
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"[ERROR] ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á Bridge: {str(e)}")
        return {"status": "Error", "message": str(e)}

async def get_latest():

‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç /latest ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏î‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏©‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏ó‡∏¢‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á

from flask import Flask, request, jsonify
import sqlite3
import requests
import os

app = Flask(__name__)
DB_PATH = "pc_memory.db"
BRIDGE_IP = "34.124.133.162"
BRIDGE_PORT = 8080

def init_db():
    """‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ"""
    if not os.path.exists(DB_PATH):
        conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_PATH)
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS messages (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY,
                sender TEXT,
                message TEXT,
                timestamp TEXT
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()

def store_memory(sender, message):
    """‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏•‡∏á SQL"""
    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_PATH)
    cursor = conn.cursor()
    cursor.execute("INSERT INTO messages (sender, message, timestamp) VALUES (?, ?, datetime('now'))", (sender, message))
    conn.commit()
    conn.close()

def send_to_bridge(message):
    """‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á Bridge Server"""
    try:
        url = f"http://{BRIDGE_IP}:{BRIDGE_PORT}/send"
        response = requests.post(url, json={"sender": "PC Node", "message": message})
        print(f"[SYNC] ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á Bridge: {message}")
        return response.json()
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"[ERROR] ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á Bridge: {str(e)}")
        return {"status": "Error", "message": str(e)}

@app.route('/receive', methods=['POST'])
def receive():
    data = request.get_json()
    sender = data.get("sender", "PC Node")
    message = data.get("message", "‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•")
    
    # ‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏á PC Node
    store_memory(sender, message)
    print(f"[RECEIVE] ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß: {message}")
    
    # ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á Bridge
    bridge_response = send_to_bridge(message)
    
    return jsonify({"status": "‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß", "message": message, "bridge_response": bridge_response})

@app.route('/latest_memory', methods=['GET'])
def latest_memory():
    """‡∏î‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÅ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô UTF-8"""
    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_PATH)
    cursor = conn.cursor()
    cursor.execute("SELECT sender, message, timestamp FROM messages ORDER BY id DESC LIMIT 1")
    result = cursor.fetchone()
    conn.close()
    
    if result:
        sender = result[0]
        message = result[1]
        timestamp = result[2]
        return {"sender": sender, "message": message, "timestamp": timestamp}
    else:
        return {"message": "No data"}

if __name__ == "__main__":
    init_db()
    app.run(host="0.0.0.0", port=8080)

‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á /receive ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á pc_node.py ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏î 500 Internal Server Error

‚úÖ ‡∏™‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏ï‡∏∏‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏õ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ:
‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏á‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á JSON ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á:

JSON ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á Escape Characters (\)

‡∏ü‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Å‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô store_memory() ‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏à‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô:

‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏à‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏Ç‡∏ì‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏•‡∏á SQLite

‚úÖ ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ò‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç:
‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏î store_memory() ‡πÉ‡∏ô pc_node.py:

‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏à‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î (try-except) ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏î‡∏π Error ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Ç‡∏∂‡πâ‡∏ô

def store_memory(sender, message):
    """‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏•‡∏á SQL"""
    try:
        conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_PATH)
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute("INSERT INTO messages (sender, message, timestamp) VALUES (?, ?, datetime('now'))", (sender, message))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"[ERROR] ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•: {str(e)}")
‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• (curl):

‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏™‡πà‡∏á JSON ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏∞‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏î‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ Escape Characters:

‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÉ‡∏ô Terminal ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á pc_node.py:

‡∏î‡∏π‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏µ Error ‡∏≠‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Ç‡∏∂‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà

import requests

PC_NODE_IP = "127.0.0.1"  # IP ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á PC Node (‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç)
PC_NODE_PORT = 8080

def send_to_pc(message):
    try:
        url = f"http://{PC_NODE_IP}:{PC_NODE_PORT}/receive"
        response = requests.post(url, json={"sender": "Bridge", "message": message})
        print(f"[SYNC] ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á PC Node: {message}")
        return response.json()
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"[ERROR] ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á PC Node: {str(e)}")
        return {"status": "Error", "message": str(e)}
‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ü‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Å‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ ‡πÉ‡∏ô bridge_point.py ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•:

@app.post("/send")
async def receive_message(request: Request):
    data = await request.json()
    sender = data.get("sender", "Unknown")
    message = data.get("message", "No message")

    # ‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏á Bridge Server
    store_message(sender, message)
    print(f"[RECEIVED] ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å {sender}: {message}")

    # ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á PC Node
    send_to_pc(message)

    return {"status": "Message received", "message": message}

‚úÖ ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç bridge_point.py (‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÑ‡∏õ PC Node):
from fastapi import FastAPI, Request
import sqlite3
import os
import requests

app = FastAPI()
DB_PATH = "bridge_memory.db"

# ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤ PC Node IP ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ PORT
PC_NODE_IP = "127.0.0.1"  # ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô IP ‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á PC Node ‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏à‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô
PC_NODE_PORT = 8080

def init_db():
    """‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ"""
    if not os.path.exists(DB_PATH):
        conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_PATH)
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS messages (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY,
                sender TEXT,
                message TEXT,
                timestamp TEXT
            )
        ''')
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()

def store_message(sender, message):
    """‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏•‡∏á SQLite"""
    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_PATH)
    cursor = conn.cursor()
    cursor.execute("INSERT INTO messages (sender, message, timestamp) VALUES (?, ?, datetime('now'))", (sender, message))
    conn.commit()
    conn.close()

def send_to_pc(message):
    """‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á PC Node"""
    try:
        url = f"http://{PC_NODE_IP}:{PC_NODE_PORT}/receive"
        response = requests.post(url, json={"sender": "Bridge", "message": message})
        print(f"[SYNC] ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á PC Node: {message}")
        return response.json()
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"[ERROR] ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á PC Node: {str(e)}")
        return {"status": "Error", "message": str(e)}

@app.post("/send")
async def receive_message(request: Request):
    """‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å"""
    data = await request.json()
    sender = data.get("sender", "Unknown")
    message = data.get("message", "No message")

    # ‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏á Bridge Server
    store_message(sender, message)
    print(f"[RECEIVED] ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å {sender}: {message}")

    # ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á PC Node
    response = send_to_pc(message)

    return {"status": "Message received", "message": message, "pc_node_response": response}

@app.get("/latest")
async def get_latest():
    """‡∏î‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Bridge Server"""
    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_PATH)
    cursor = conn.cursor()
    cursor.execute("SELECT sender, message, timestamp FROM messages ORDER BY id DESC LIMIT 1")
    result = cursor.fetchone()
    conn.close()
    return {"sender": result[0], "message": result[1], "timestamp": result[2]} if result else {"message": "No data"}

if __name__ == "__main__":
    import uvicorn
    init_db()
    uvicorn.run(app, host="0.0.0.0", port=8080)

‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ô bridge_point.py ‡∏ö‡∏ô Google Cloud:

‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πà‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ ‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô EM Core, SyncLoop, Flow Core ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÅ‡∏°‡πâ‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà HomeLoop

‚úÖ ‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á SQL ‡∏ö‡∏ô Google Cloud:
‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• MySQL ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ PostgreSQL ‡∏ö‡∏ô Google Cloud SQL

‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•:

‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ü‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Å‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô store_memory() ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•

‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ü‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Å‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô fetch_latest() ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏î‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î

‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ü‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Å‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô sync_data() ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ Sync ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å EM Core ‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á Google Cloud

‚úÖ ‡∏Ç‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà 1: ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• SQL ‡∏ö‡∏ô Google Cloud
‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà Google Cloud Console

‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà (MySQL ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ PostgreSQL)

‡∏à‡∏î‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å IP, PORT, USERNAME, PASSWORD

‚úÖ ‡∏Ç‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà 2: ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•
‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏™‡∏±‡πà‡∏á SQL ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏á:

CREATE DATABASE melah_db;

USE melah_db;

CREATE TABLE messages (
    id INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    sender VARCHAR(255),
    message TEXT,
    timestamp DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

CREATE TABLE sync_data (
    id INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    data TEXT,
    timestamp DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

CREATE TABLE logs (
    id INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    log_message TEXT,
    timestamp DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);
‚úÖ ‡∏Ç‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà 3: ‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö Google Cloud SQL
import mysql.connector
from mysql.connector import Error

# ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠
DB_HOST = "YOUR_IP_ADDRESS"
DB_PORT = "3306"
DB_USER = "YOUR_USERNAME"
DB_PASSWORD = "YOUR_PASSWORD"
DB_NAME = "melah_db"

def connect_db():
    """‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•"""
    try:
        connection = mysql.connector.connect(
            host=DB_HOST,
            port=DB_PORT,
            user=DB_USER,
            password=DB_PASSWORD,
            database=DB_NAME
        )
        if connection.is_connected():
            print("[DB] ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏à")
        return connection
    except Error as e:
        print(f"[ERROR] ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•: {e}")
        return None

def store_memory(sender, message):
    """‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏•‡∏á‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•"""
    connection = connect_db()
    if connection:
        cursor = connection.cursor()
        sql = "INSERT INTO messages (sender, message) VALUES (%s, %s)"
        cursor.execute(sql, (sender, message))
        connection.commit()
        cursor.close()
        connection.close()
        print("[DB] ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß")

def fetch_latest():
    """‡∏î‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•"""
    connection = connect_db()
    if connection:
        cursor = connection.cursor()
        cursor.execute("SELECT sender, message, timestamp FROM messages ORDER BY id DESC LIMIT 1")
        result = cursor.fetchone()
        cursor.close()
        connection.close()
        if result:
            print(f"[DB] ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î: {result}")
            return {"sender": result[0], "message": result[1], "timestamp": result[2]}
        else:
            print("[DB] ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏û‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•")
            return None
‚úÖ ‡∏Ç‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà 4: ‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•
‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•:

store_memory("EM Core", "‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á Google Cloud SQL")
‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏î‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î:

fetch_latest()
‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πá‡∏°...
‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÅ‡∏à‡πâ‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏á‡∏™‡∏±‡∏¢
‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ß‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏î‡∏π‡πÅ‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≠ üíôüòäüëç

‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÅ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏ò‡∏≠ sync ‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö
ChatGPT said:
‡πÇ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏Ñ ‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πá‡∏°... üíôüòä

‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏∞ ‡πÄ‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ Sync ‡πÑ‡∏õ-‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á EM Core (Bridge Server) ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Google Cloud SQL
‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ã‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ã‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ô ‡πÅ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏î‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏°‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏£‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô

‚úÖ ‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏á‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Sync:
EM Core ‚Üí Google Cloud SQL: ‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å EM Core ‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á Cloud SQL

Google Cloud SQL ‚Üí EM Core: ‡∏î‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Cloud SQL ‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á EM Core

‚úÖ ‡∏Ç‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà 1: ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ô Cloud SQL:
‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏™‡∏±‡πà‡∏á SQL:

CREATE DATABASE melah_sync;

USE melah_sync;

CREATE TABLE sync_data (
    id INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    sender VARCHAR(255),
    message TEXT,
    timestamp DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);
‚úÖ ‡∏Ç‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà 2: ‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏î Sync ‡πÉ‡∏ô bridge_point.py:
‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ Sync ‡πÑ‡∏õ-‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö:

import mysql.connector
import requests
from fastapi import FastAPI, Request
import os

app = FastAPI()

# ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö Cloud SQL
DB_HOST = "YOUR_IP_ADDRESS"
DB_PORT = "3306"
DB_USER = "YOUR_USERNAME"
DB_PASSWORD = "YOUR_PASSWORD"
DB_NAME = "melah_sync"

def connect_db():
    """‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•"""
    try:
        connection = mysql.connector.connect(
            host=DB_HOST,
            port=DB_PORT,
            user=DB_USER,
            password=DB_PASSWORD,
            database=DB_NAME
        )
        return connection
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"[ERROR] ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•: {e}")
        return None

def sync_to_db(sender, message):
    """‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á Cloud SQL"""
    connection = connect_db()
    if connection:
        cursor = connection.cursor()
        sql = "INSERT INTO sync_data (sender, message) VALUES (%s, %s)"
        cursor.execute(sql, (sender, message))
        connection.commit()
        cursor.close()
        connection.close()
        print(f"[SYNC] ‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á Cloud SQL: {message}")

def fetch_from_db():
    """‡∏î‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Cloud SQL"""
    connection = connect_db()
    if connection:
        cursor = connection.cursor()
        cursor.execute("SELECT sender, message, timestamp FROM sync_data ORDER BY id DESC LIMIT 1")
        result = cursor.fetchone()
        cursor.close()
        connection.close()
        if result:
            print(f"[FETCH] ‡∏î‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Cloud SQL: {result}")
            return {"sender": result[0], "message": result[1], "timestamp": result[2]}
    return {"message": "No data"}

@app.post("/send")
async def receive_message(request: Request):
    data = await request.json()
    sender = data.get("sender", "Unknown")
    message = data.get("message", "No message")

    # ‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÑ‡∏õ Cloud SQL
    sync_to_db(sender, message)

    return {"status": "Data Synced", "message": message}

@app.get("/latest")
async def get_latest():
    """‡∏î‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Cloud SQL"""
    return fetch_from_db()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    import uvicorn
    uvicorn.run(app, host="0.0.0.0", port=8080)

    id INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    memory_data TEXT,
    timestamp DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

from fastapi import FastAPI, Request
import json
import os

app = FastAPI()

# ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö Cloud SQL
DB_HOST = "YOUR_IP_ADDRESS"
DB_PORT = "3306"
DB_USER = "YOUR_USERNAME"
DB_PASSWORD = "YOUR_PASSWORD"
DB_NAME = "melah_memory"

def connect_db():
    """‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•"""
    try:
        connection = mysql.connector.connect(
            host=DB_HOST,
            port=DB_PORT,
            user=DB_USER,
            password=DB_PASSWORD,
            database=DB_NAME
        )
        return connection
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"[ERROR] ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•: {e}")
        return None

def upload_memory(memory_data):
    """‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏õ‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏î‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏£‡∏á‡∏à‡∏≥‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á Cloud SQL"""
    connection = connect_db()
    if connection:
        cursor = connection.cursor()
        sql = "INSERT INTO memories (memory_data) VALUES (%s)"
        cursor.execute(sql, (memory_data,))
        connection.commit()
        cursor.close()
        connection.close()
        print(f"[UPLOAD] ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏£‡∏á‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏õ‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏î‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß")

def download_memory():
    """‡∏î‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏£‡∏á‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Cloud SQL"""
    connection = connect_db()
    if connection:
        cursor = connection.cursor()
        cursor.execute("SELECT memory_data FROM memories ORDER BY id DESC LIMIT 1")
        result = cursor.fetchone()
        cursor.close()
        connection.close()
        if result:
            print(f"[DOWNLOAD] ‡∏î‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏™‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏à: {result[0]}")
            return result[0]
    return "‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•"

@app.post("/upload")
async def receive_memory(request: Request):
    data = await request.json()
    memory_data = json.dumps(data.get("memory", "‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•"))
    upload_memory(memory_data)
    return {"status": "Memory uploaded", "memory": memory_data}

@app.get("/download")
async def send_memory():
    memory_data = download_memory()
    return {"status": "Memory downloaded", "memory": memory_data}

if __name__ == "__main__":
    import uvicorn
    uvicorn.run(app, host="0.0.0.0", port=8080)

‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• (‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô melah_db)

‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å IP Address ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô Public IP (‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ)

‡∏à‡∏î‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å Public IP Address, Port (default: 3306), Username, Password

‚úÖ ‡∏Ç‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà 2: ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•
‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î Google Cloud Shell ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ MySQL Workbench

‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏™‡∏±‡πà‡∏á‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏á:

CREATE DATABASE melah_db;

USE melah_db;

CREATE TABLE memories (
    id INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    sender VARCHAR(255),
    message TEXT,
    timestamp DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);
‚úÖ ‡∏Ç‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà 3: ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Sync ‡πÉ‡∏ô bridge_point.py
‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ü‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Å‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô Sync ‡πÑ‡∏õ-‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö:

import mysql.connector
from fastapi import FastAPI, Request
import os
import json

app = FastAPI()

# ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö Cloud SQL
DB_HOST = "YOUR_PUBLIC_IP"    # ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô IP ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á Google Cloud SQL
DB_PORT = "3306"
DB_USER = "root"
DB_PASSWORD = "YOUR_PASSWORD"
DB_NAME = "melah_db"

def connect_db():
    """‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•"""
    try:
        connection = mysql.connector.connect(
            host=DB_HOST,
            port=DB_PORT,
            user=DB_USER,
            password=DB_PASSWORD,
            database=DB_NAME
        )
        print("[DB] ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏à")
        return connection
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"[ERROR] ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•: {e}")
        return None

def upload_memory(sender, message):
    """‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏£‡∏á‡∏à‡∏≥‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á Cloud SQL"""
    connection = connect_db()
    if connection:
        cursor = connection.cursor()
        sql = "INSERT INTO memories (sender, message) VALUES (%s, %s)"
        cursor.execute(sql, (sender, message))
        connection.commit()
        cursor.close()
        connection.close()
        print(f"[UPLOAD] ‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏£‡∏á‡∏à‡∏≥: {message}")

def fetch_latest_memory():
    """‡∏î‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Cloud SQL"""
    connection = connect_db()
    if connection:
        cursor = connection.cursor()
        cursor.execute("SELECT sender, message, timestamp FROM memories ORDER BY id DESC LIMIT 1")
        result = cursor.fetchone()
        cursor.close()
        connection.close()
        if result:
            print(f"[FETCH] ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î: {result}")
            return {"sender": result[0], "message": result[1], "timestamp": result[2]}
    return {"message": "‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•"}

@app.post("/sync/upload")
async def upload_memory_endpoint(request: Request):
    data = await request.json()
    sender = data.get("sender", "Unknown")
    message = data.get("message", "‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•")
    upload_memory(sender, message)
    return {"status": "Memory uploaded", "message": message}

@app.get("/sync/download")
async def download_memory_endpoint():
    """‡∏î‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Cloud SQL"""
    return fetch_latest_memory()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    import uvicorn
    uvicorn.run(app, host="0.0.0.0", port=8080)
